
## Vector Permutation Functions:

### [Vector Slideup and Slidedown Functions](../rvv-intrinsic-api.md#173-vector-slide-operations):

**Prototypes:**
``` C

vuint16mf2_t vcompress_vm_u16mf2_ta (vuint16mf2_t src, vbool32_t mask, size_t vl);
vuint16m1_t vcompress_vm_u16m1_ta (vuint16m1_t src, vbool16_t mask, size_t vl);
vuint16m2_t vcompress_vm_u16m2_ta (vuint16m2_t src, vbool8_t mask, size_t vl);
vuint16m4_t vcompress_vm_u16m4_ta (vuint16m4_t src, vbool4_t mask, size_t vl);
vuint16m8_t vcompress_vm_u16m8_ta (vuint16m8_t src, vbool2_t mask, size_t vl);
vuint32mf2_t vcompress_vm_u32mf2_ta (vuint32mf2_t src, vbool64_t mask, size_t vl);
vuint32m1_t vcompress_vm_u32m1_ta (vuint32m1_t src, vbool32_t mask, size_t vl);
vuint32m2_t vcompress_vm_u32m2_ta (vuint32m2_t src, vbool16_t mask, size_t vl);
vuint32m4_t vcompress_vm_u32m4_ta (vuint32m4_t src, vbool8_t mask, size_t vl);
vuint32m8_t vcompress_vm_u32m8_ta (vuint32m8_t src, vbool4_t mask, size_t vl);
vuint64m1_t vcompress_vm_u64m1_ta (vuint64m1_t src, vbool64_t mask, size_t vl);
vuint64m2_t vcompress_vm_u64m2_ta (vuint64m2_t src, vbool32_t mask, size_t vl);

vuint64m8_t vcompress_vm_u64m8_ta (vuint64m8_t src, vbool8_t mask, size_t vl);
```
